<time>1602313264981<//time><rating>1</rating>< Text>
I've visited the shop several times from the past week to several years ago and every time these guys act so shady. I negotiated the price of a piece over the phone 2 years ago and when I came the next day to purchase it they wouldn't honor the agreed upon price. The employee, a middle age gentlemen even used explicit language to try and intimidate me when I told them they were not honoring the negotiated price. Fast forward to a week ago, I negotiated a price online for a dab tool and when I got there they changed the price again, on a measly item under $30! Two days ago I went by and asked some questions regarding inventory. The employee that was working acted like I was an inconvenience to him and would vaguely answer my questions. Each time I had a bad experience here I would tell myself that its probably just a one off, but after 3 times it seems to be the S.O.P. They seem to judge people by their appearance and how much money they perceive someone can spend than treating their customers equally. Its a shame because out of all the shops in San Diego, they carry the nicest glass. I have resorted to conducting my glass purchases online from shops out of the city. Every single time I felt like the employees respected me, unlike at this shop. Unless you want to come in looking like a million bucks and ready to spend it, save your time. These guys judge a book by its cover and try to one up people on the daily.< /Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Great place for all your smoking needs! They have an incredible supply of glass for all types of smokers, great price range too!! The staff is knowledgeable and always helps me pick a piece to fit my needs.

I have bought straight pipes, bubblers, water pipes with and without percolators, cigars, hookahs, hookah tobacco, vaporizers, etc and have always been happy with my purchase as well as with the price!

Parking on Garnet is a little tough but you usually get lucky and park on their block or close to it. There's also paid parking nearby. The whole area is cool to check out too, tons of food and drink and the beach is very close!<//review>

<Date>1555125884625< /Date><Rating>4</Rating><Review>It was closed the day I visited, but from the other reviews it looks like I didn't miss much. Almost all the exhibits are outside the locked doors and are available to view in the zoology building. Some had information, most just a name. I loved seeing the Tyrannosaurus up close. There were several other skulls and a few other skeletons. Another highlight for me was the cast of Lucy, the hominid found by Dr Leaky and his team that inspired so many people's interest in anthropology. It isn't a very big place, and as interested as I was, I only spent a couple of hours. Several tour groups came through spending more like 10 or 15 minutes. It's a place to visit if you are interested and near the campus, but I wouldn't call it a destination into itself.</Review>< Pics>

< review>
I was just driving through and decided to stop and see the place.  I’m glad I did.  I’m not sure why they don’t allow photos of the interior but there were signs everywhere saying it wasn’t allowed.

The selection of international products was impressive and completely unexpected (candy, drinks, ramen, cookies and snacks from all over the world).

I ordered half a sandwich and it was fantastic.  The portions are huge and everything was fresh (Turkey, provolone, lettuce, tomato, bread, mustard, horseradish and pickles).

If you’re in the area, definitely recommend stopping in for a sandwich.<//review>

We come here after a day at the Kern River Preserve. It's a throwback to the old fashion general store with a few extras. The candy selection is out of this world. They have candy that you haven't seen since you were a child. It's fresh and reasonably priced. After that go to the back of the store for a really good deli sandwich! This isn't Subway, this is a huge sandwich (we split one between us). its worth the drive and you can go to the Preserve and picnic there. Check it out while your there and give a donation, they need it and it's a good cause.<//review>

<Review>Their sandwiches are delicious and served with choice of home made potato or macaroni salad, a pickle and a small bag of chips. The pickled eggs are great. They carry a large variety of bottled root beer from all over. We found one of our favorite root bears from Arizona there, Route 66 Root Beer. This was a treat. Lots of candy to choose from, from all around the world. Old Fashion Favorites not found in most places. Including a large selection of sugar free and "penny candy". A very large selection of loose and bagged teas. Unique gifts, cards, stationary and assorted household items can be found here. My daughter loves that they give $2 bills in your change. This is a rare treat for her. The woman that runs the place is so sweet and kind. She seems to always have a positive sweet attitude towards all her customers. The flowers are in bloom this time of year an make for a great photo opportunity outside. **They have scales here to weigh your vehicle for DMV purposes. This is great for people that would ordinarily have to travel outside the valley. I'm glad The Onyx Store is still in business and is being run so well. The old wood floors have seen a lot of travelers over the years. The history here is amazing. Enjoy the garden out back to enjoy your lunch.</Review>< date>

<Review>I have been coming to this car wash ever since I have been driving, about 16 years now. I remember when they used to have gas pumps here. I have since moved but when I get a chance visiting family I come and get my vehicles washed here because they usually do a good job.
On 2/10/16 I went to get my new truck cleaned before my grandmother's funeral which was the next day. I took a picture of the truck on the line because it was its first time here. After snapping the picture, I notice the truck hopping. The washers yell and whistle then the driver runs and jumps back into my truck and it starts rolling smoothly. The washer turns around and makes a face like whoops we f*$cked up.
I then realize that the driver had left my truck in drive and that is why it was hopping when the rollers were trying to push it. Worried about my drivetrain being damaged I went to the cashier to complain and to speak to something in charge. I wanted them to document it just incase the truck would not drive in the same manner as before.
This man comes out from the back office and I explain to him what happened. I see him talking to the driver from the window. I ask if I could speak to the owner just to make sure it was documented that they did not have my truck in neutral when it went down the line. She gave me a card with a manager name that had been whited out and a person named Sunny written in place. She said to leave my name and number and I would be called on 2/11/16. Its 2/13/16 and still no call and I figured as much.
Just wanted to warn anybody taking their vehicle here to watch it when it goes down the line.;
My truck veers slightly to the left now but I will call them Monday and try to speak to this Sunny. Don't waste your hard earned money here and risk your vehicle for people that are not careful with it.
To top it off before I left I found the person in the office and he was joking and laughing with his workers in the detailing bay and I asked him what happened. He said the guy left it in gear and then walked away. One of the worst customer experiences I have encountered.< /Review>< date>
